Are there any strict grammar mistakes in my sentence? Yes or No. 2. If yes, what grammar mistakes do you see? Explain them. If there's no mistakes, write 'None' 3. What is the correct version of the sentence? Write it like 'sentence', please. If there are no errors in my sentence, just write it again in ' marks like 'sentence'
    ASSISTANT:
    1. No, I don't see any strict grammar mistakes in your sentence. However, there is a minor lexical mistake that can be improved.
    2. The word "which" should be replaced with "that." This is because "which" is used to introduce a clause or a situation, while "that" is used to introduce an essential clause or information that defines the noun it precedes. In your sentence, "which you gave me" is not essential information about the book; rather, it's just additional information about who gave the book to you.
    3. Here's the corrected version of your sentence: I like the book that you gave me.

    2. The subject-verb agreement is incorrect. "That banana" is singular and should be matched with a singular verb, but "eating" is a plural verb form. Additionally, the word order of the sentence is not natural. It would sound more normal to say "The monkey is eating the banana."
    3. The correct version of the sentence is: The monkey is eating the banana.
